***добро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро</a> (1585)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dòbrъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobró</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добра́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>the good</li>
<li>goods, property</li>
<li>stuff</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> green light, consent, permission
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показ.html>пока́з</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льма</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Komitét dal <b>dobró</b> na pokáz nóvovo fílʹma.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The committee has given the go-ahead for screening the new film.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobró</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>okay</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>kindly</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dóbryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добровольный.html>доброво́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobrovólʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>voluntary, of one's free will
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:добровольный.html>доброво́льных</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:начало.html>нача́лах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>dobrovólʹnyx</b> načálax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on voluntary lines, on a voluntary basis</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:добровольный.html>доброво́льные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожертвование.html>поже́ртвования</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>dobrovólʹnyje</b> požértvovanija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">by voluntary donations</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добродетель.html>доброде́тель</a> (12625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> (<i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">добръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobrŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">дѣтѣль</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dětělĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὐεργεσία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">euergesía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродетель.html>доброде́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobrodételʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродетель.html>доброде́тели</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродетель.html>доброде́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродетель.html>доброде́телей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>virtue (excellence in morals)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добродушие.html>доброду́шие</a> (20929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродушие.html>доброду́шие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobrodúšije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродушие.html>доброду́шия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродушие.html>доброду́шия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродушие.html>доброду́ший</a></b>)

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***добродушный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добродушный.html>доброду́шный</a> (7011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">добродꙋшьнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobrodušĭnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobro</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дꙋша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">duša</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soul</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ьнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ĭnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὔψυχος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eúpsukhos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Also, compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродушный.html>доброду́шен</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobrodušen</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">добродушан</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">dobrodušný</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">dobroduszny</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добродушный.html>доброду́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobrodúšnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>good-natured</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́ш</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><b>доб<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вест.html>вест</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доброта.html>доброта́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobrotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доброта.html>доброты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>доб<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>ро́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>добротнее, добротней.</i>

***добрый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добрый</a> (515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">добръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobrŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dobrъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dóbryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)добре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:добреть.html>добре́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрейший.html>добре́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>kind, good, genial</li>
<li>kindly, good-hearted</li>
<li>gracious, nice</li>
<li>gentle, soft</li>
<li>decent</li>
<li>benign</li>
<li>beneficent</li>
<li>tenderhearted</li>
<li>good-natured</li>
<li>kindhearted, warm-hearted</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> good, solid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брых</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:километр.html>киломе́тров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí <b>dóbryx</b> désjatʹ kilométrov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to walk a good/solid ten kilometres</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>до́б<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>рый</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>добре́е, <a href = vnd.unilang:добреть.html>добре́й</a>, подобре́е, <a href = vnd.unilang:подобреть.html>подобре́й</a>.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-добр-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***добывание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добывание.html>добыва́ние</a> (20335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добывать.html>добыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добывание.html>добыва́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobyvánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добывание.html>добыва́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добывание.html>добыва́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добывание.html>добыва́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>getting, procuring</li>
<li>extraction, mining</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добывать.html>добыва́ть</a> (4955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добыть.html>добы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добывать.html>добыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добыть.html>добы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to obtain, to get, to procure</li>
<li>to extract, to mine, to quarry</li>
<li>to bag <i>hunt</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***добыча.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́ча</a> (3720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dobyťa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dobýča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>extraction, mining, quarrying
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́ча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нефть.html>не́фти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dobýča</b> néfti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">oil production</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́ча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>угля́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dobýča</b> ugljá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">coal production</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>booty, spoil, plunder <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">plunder taken from an enemy in time of war, or seized by piracy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принести.html>принёс</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценный.html>це́нную</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́чу</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On prinjós cénnuju <b>dobýču</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He has brought some valuable <b>booty</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>prey, catch <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something which is captured or caught</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:добыча.html>добы́чей</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">statʹ <b>dobýčej</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall prey (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>доведённый</a> (3083)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>доведённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dovedjónnyj</span>)
